class=\"end\">\n<li>TikTok has reportedly chosen a buyer for its U.S, Australian, and New Zealand businesses.</li>\n<li>With Microsoft in the running, a deal could be announced \"as soon as come to an end soon, according to a new report. <a href=\"https://www.cnbc.com/2020/08/31/tiktok-deal-to-sell-us-business-could-be-announced-as-soon-as-tomorrow.html\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">CNBC</a> reports that TikTok has selected a buyer for its U.S., Australian, and New Zealand businesses. An announcement for the deal could come \"as soon as Tuesday,\" the report notes.</p>\n\n<p>Microsoft, Walmart, and Oracle are all in the mix as potential owners. Microsoft acknowledged it was seeking to purchase TikTok earlier this month, while Walmart said last week that it was <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/microsoft-may-have-surprising-bid-partner-its-pursuit-tiktok\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">partnering with Microsoft</a> on a bid. Should the Microsoft-Walmart partnership succeed, it would make Walmart a minority owner with a deal worth between $20 billion and $30 billion, CNBC notes.</p>\n\n<p>The sale could hit a snag, however. Last week, the Chinese government put TikTok's AI tech on a technology export list. The result is TikTok owner ByteDance would need a <a href=\"https://www.cnbc.com/2020/08/31/tiktok-sale-bytedance-says-it-will-abide-by-amended-china-export-rules.html\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">license from the Chinese government</a> to sell TikTok to any U.S. business.</p>\n\n<p>Reporting <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/microsoft-likely-purchase-tiktok-within-next-48-hours\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">emerged last week</a> that a TikTok sale was imminent. The deal is on a strict timeline after an <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/tiktok-files-lawsuit-against-trump-administration-over-ban\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">executive order from the Trump administration</a> dictated that TikTok must either be sold or it will be banned. TikTok has since sued the U.S. government, stating that the executive order was rushed out without giving TikTok a chance to defend itself against claims that it is a security threat.</p>\n\n<p>Last week, TikTok CEO Kevin Mayer <a href=\"https://www.windowscentral.com/tiktok-ceo-kevin-mayer-steps-down-apps-future-remains-uncertain\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">stepped down from his role</a>, citing the changing political environment as a reason for his departure. cost?</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/samsung-galaxy-s20\" title=\"Samsung Galaxy S20: Everything you need to know!\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large_wm_brw/public/article_images/2020/02/samsung-galaxy-s20-ultra-bader-1.jpg?itok=9Aj6MZ4O\" /></a></p> \n   <p>Now that we've reached the end of this guide, it's time to talk about everyone's favorite subject — price.</p> \n   <p>The Galaxy S20, S20+, and S20 Ultra have starting prices of $1,000, $1,200, and $1,400, respectively. As of March 6, all three phones are <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/best-places-buy-galaxy-s20-less\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">available for purchase</a>.</p> \n   <p>You can pick up the S20 at most major carriers and retailers in the U.S., with many of them offering generous promotions and discounts to help you save some cash. Right now, Samsung is offering up to a $500 instant credit when you trade-in an eligible device.</p> \n   <p>Outside of Samsung, you'll also find deals from Amazon, Verizon, T-Mobile, and plenty more. The S20 lineup is undoubtedly expensive, but if you know where to look, it's fairly easy to save a <em>lot</em> of money.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"handson\">First thing's first, check out our Galaxy S20 reviews!</h2> \n   <div class=\"article-body__video\">\n    <div class=\"video_iframe\">\n     <iframe src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/SRkK6lKu3cw?modestbranding=0&amp;html5=1&amp;rel=0&amp;autoplay=0&amp;wmode=opaque&amp;loop=0&amp;controls=1&amp;autohide=0&amp;showinfo=0&amp;theme=dark&amp;color=red&amp;enablejsapi=1\" width=\"682\" height=\"400\" class=\"video-filter video-youtube vf-srkk6lku3cw\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"true\" loading=\"lazy\"></iframe>\n    </div>\n   </div> \n   <!--/video--> \n   <p>Before you dive too deep into this guide, a good place to start is by checking out our full reviews of the S20 lineup.</p> \n   <p>As you'd probably expect, the <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/samsung-galaxy-s20-ultra-review\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">S20 Ultra</a> is a <em>really</em> good phone. Its 120Hz AMOLED display is a thing of beauty, Samsung's build quality is as good as ever, and the upgraded camera system is a lot of fun to shoot with. Samsung went all out with the phone, and the end result is a device that packs in just about every feature imaginable.</p> \n   <p>We don't blame you for wanting an S20 Ultra of your own this very second, but keep in mind that it is not a perfect phone. The 120Hz refresh rate is a massive drain on battery life, Samsung's in-screen fingerprint sensor is a pain to use, and there's no getting around the $1,400 asking price.</p> \n   <div class=\"article-body__video\">\n    <div class=\"video_iframe\">\n     <iframe src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/s5QWeYVQxD8?modestbranding=0&amp;html5=1&amp;rel=0&amp;autoplay=0&amp;wmode=opaque&amp;loop=0&amp;controls=1&amp;autohide=0&amp;showinfo=0&amp;theme=dark&amp;color=red&amp;enablejsapi=1\" width=\"682\" height=\"400\" class=\"video-filter video-youtube vf-s5qweyvqxd8\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"true\" loading=\"lazy\"></iframe>\n    </div>\n   </div> \n   <!--/video--> \n   <p>Alternatively, you could just get the <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/samsung-galaxy-s20-plus-review\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Galaxy S20+</a> . It's $200 less than the S20 Ultra while being every bit as good. The digital zooming isn't <em>quite</em> as impressive and the battery is smaller, but it's also much easier to handle thanks to its smaller size and puts a significantly lesser dent in your wallet.</p> \n   <p>Then, there's the baby <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/samsung-galaxy-s20-review\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Galaxy S20</a>. You might be inclined to think that the baseline S20 is the least exciting on the bunch, but it's actually the one we'd recommend to most people. It has the smallest price tag, is easy to use in one hand, and offers basically all of the same features of the more expensive S20+.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"models\">Which Galaxy S20 model should you buy?</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/samsung-galaxy-s20\" title=\"Samsung Galaxy S20: Everything you need to know!\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large_wm_brw/public/article_images/2020/02/galaxy-s20-all-models-grey-4.jpg?itok=KO_DzWuY\" /></a></p> \n   <p>Speaking of the different models, let's take a closer look at what each one is bringing to the table.</p> \n   <p>At their core, the S20, S20+, and S20 Ultra are very similar. All three phones have 120Hz displays, Qualcomm's Snapdragon 865 processor, expandable storage, water resistance, and wireless charging. However, similar to what we saw last year with the S10e, S10, and S10+, there are also clear differences between them.</p> \n   <p>While the S20 isn't cheap with a starting price of $1000, it is <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/samsung-galaxy-s20-plus-vs-s20\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">the lesser phone of the trio</a>. It has the fewest cameras, smallest battery, and doesn't connect to mmWave 5G networks. Then again, it's the S20 version that'll put the smallest dent in your wallet and is a good choice if you prefer phones with smaller screen sizes.</p> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/samsung-galaxy-s20-ultra-vs-s20-plus\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">In the middle of the bunch is the S20+</a>, offering modest improvements in all of the areas where it differs from the regular S20. If you step all the way up to the S20 Ultra, you're getting the biggest and baddest S20 experience possible — though it is going to cost you.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"specs\">These are all of the specs</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/samsung-galaxy-s20\" title=\"Samsung Galaxy S20: Everything you need to know!\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large_wm_brw/public/article_images/2020/02/galaxy-s20-vs-s20-plus-grey-1.jpg?itok=dlNgje5M\" /></a></p> \n   <p>Samsung doesn't mess around with specs for its Galaxy S phones, and that idea has carried over to the S20 lineup.</p> \n   <p>Whether we're talking about the S20, S20+, or S20 Ultra, these are flagship phones through and through. As such, you'll find flagship specs in just about every regard.</p> \n   <p>Here's a quick rundown of what they're packing.</p> \n   <table class=\"spec-table\"> \n    <thead> \n     <tr> \n href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/samsung-galaxy-s20-specifications\" title=\"\" class=\"cta norewrite\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">Samsung Galaxy S20 Specifications</a></p> \n   <h2 id=\"camera\">There are also big upgrades in the camera department</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/samsung-galaxy-s20\" title=\"Samsung Galaxy S20: Everything you need to know!\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large_wm_brw/public/article_images/2020/02/samsung-galaxy-s20-ultra-bader-3.jpg?itok=ofT0VP_a\" /></a></p> \n   <p>Similar to the displays, the Galaxy S20 is also being used as a showcase for <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/galaxy-s20-cameras-what-are-differences-between-models\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Samsung's improved camera tech</a>. The Galaxy S9 and S10 had fine cameras, but compared to what's been offered by the rest of the competition, Samsung's efforts in this department have felt lukewarm.</p> \n   <p>That changes with the S20 lineup, and it all starts with the S20 and S20+. Both phones still have a 12MP lens for the primary camera, but the big improvement is that the pixels are about 30% larger so that substantially more light can be let into a shot. The telephoto camera has also been upgraded, now featuring a 64MP sensor with 3x lossless zoom. If ultra-wide is more your thing, this year's sensor brings 40% larger pixels which should help in low-light scenarios.</p> \n   <div class=\"media-gallery-wrap\">\n    <div class=\"media-gallery-flat\">\n     <div data-title=\"Galaxy S20 Ultra main camera sample\" <!--/media-gallery-flat-->\n   </div> \n   <p>Those are all worthwhile improvements, but where things get really interesting is when you look at the Galaxy S20 Ultra.</p> \n   <p>It offers a massive 108MP primary camera, using pixel binning to take pictures that come out as 12MP shots. There's also a 48MP telephoto camera, and because of the way it's positioned inside of the 20 Ultra, it's able to offer 10x lossless zoom and up to 100x digital zoom if you want to go all out.</p> \n   <p>Above, you'll see <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/here-are-our-first-samsung-galaxy-s20-camera-samples\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">a selection of pictures we've taken</a> with the S20 Ultra. We could go on and on about getting into the specifics, but the tl;dr is that photos look really, really good. With the main sensor, specifically, we're seeing significant improvements with detail and natural bokeh thanks to the huge sensor size. Samsung's processing still has a tendency to be too heavy-handed with things like HDR and highlights, but overall, we've been impressed.</p> \n   <blockquote class=\"twitter-tweet\">\n    <p lang=\"en\" dir=\"ltr\">Another great example of the <a href=\"https://twitter.com/SamsungMobileUS?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">@SamsungMobileUS</a> <a href=\"https://twitter.com/hashtag/GalaxyS20Ultra?src=hash&amp;ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">#GalaxyS20Ultra</a> Space Zoom! Thankfully, it doesn't have to be. We've spent a lot of quality time with all models of the S20, ensuring we can keep you in the loop on how to get the most out of the phones.</p> \n   <p>For starters, you'll want to know how to do all of the basics on the S20 — whether that's <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/how-quickly-access-notifications-galaxy-s20\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">accessing your notifications</a>, <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/how-enable-dark-mode-galaxy-s20\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">enabling dark mode</a>, or <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/how-change-and-edit-camera-modes-galaxy-s20\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">customizing the various camera modes</a>. These are all small things on their own, but once you learn to master them all, you'll be able to have the S20 work for you rather than against you.</p> \n   <p>There are also some more specific features to play around with, such as <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/how-change-galaxy-s20-refresh-rate-120hz-or-60hz\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">changing the Galaxy S20's refresh rate</a>. The 120Hz mode looks absolutely gorgeous, but because it's refreshing at twice the speed of 60Hz, it also uses a lot more battery. By switching back and forth between these two modes, you can choose to favor performance or battery life whenever you please.</p> \n   <p>Another great feature is <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/how-turn-live-caption-galaxy-s20\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Live Caption</a>, which uses on-device tech to display captions for any audio or video that's playing from your Galaxy S20. Not only is it great from an accessibility standpoint, but it can also be really convenient if you're trying to watch a YouTube video in private and don't want to rely on YouTube's generally awful closed captioning.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"upgrade\">Should you upgrade from an older Galaxy phone?</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/samsung-galaxy-s20\" title=\"Samsung Galaxy S20: Everything you need to know!\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large_wm_brw/public/article_images/2019/02/galaxy-s10-s10-plus-s10e-all-white.jpg?itok=7GhO4guC\" /></a></p> \n   <p>There's no denying that the S20 lineup is mighty impressive, but if you already have an older Galaxy phone, do you really need to upgrade? Samsung builds its phones to last, so if you have an <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/samsung-galaxy-s20-vs-galaxy-s10\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">S10</a> or <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/samsung-galaxy-s20-vs-galaxy-s9\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">S9</a>, chances are you can probably hold onto it for a little while longer and be just fine.</p> \n   <p>On the flip side, when you take into consideration all of the upgrades offered by the S20, there's also an argument to be made as to why you should upgrade. The 120Hz display is a big deal, the camera improvements are nothing to scoff at, and you get ample future-proofing with the Snapdragon 865, minimum of 12GB of RAM, etc.</p> \n   <p>Ultimately, it comes down to whether or not you're happy with your current Galaxy handset and how much you value the upgrades offered by the Galaxy S20.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"compare\">How the S20 lineup compares to other handsets</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/samsung-galaxy-s20\" title=\"Samsung Galaxy S20: Everything you need to know!\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large_wm_brw/public/article_images/2020/05/galaxy-s20-plus-oneplus-8.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>In that same breath, it's also worth pitting the Galaxy S20 up against phones from other manufacturers. Samsung is far from the only company making quality smartphones, meaning the S20 needs to make an argument as to why you should buy it over everything else being offered.</p> \n   <p>Looking at the regular S20, it has some stiff competition <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/oneplus-8-vs-galaxy-s20\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">coming from the OnePlus 8</a>. While you do give up on some features like wireless charging and water resistance with OnePlus's phone, you end up with a very similar experience for hundreds of dollars less. Especially in a market that's incredibly price-conscious right now, that's a big deal. There's a similar argument to be made when <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/oneplus-8-pro-vs-galaxy-s20-plus\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">comparing the Galaxy S20+ and OnePlus 8 Pro</a>, as you still have a sizeable price difference even with the Pro's added features and improved cameras over the regular OnePlus 8.</p> \n   <p>And, of course, we have to talk about how the Galaxy S20 Ultra compares against <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/samsung-galaxy-note-20-ultra-vs-galaxy-s20-ultra\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Samsung's own Note 20 Ultra</a>. Both phones brandish the Ultra name and have two of the highest price tags around, though it's pretty clear to us which of them is the better buy.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"colors\">Five colors are up for grabs this year</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/samsung-galaxy-s20\" title=\"Samsung Galaxy S20: Everything you need to know!\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large_wm_brw/public/article_images/2020/02/galaxy-s20-group-three-colors-1.jpg?itok=do4DJYn5\" /></a></p> \n   <p>Samsung has been known to offer some truly great colors for its smartphones, and that's <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/which-color-galaxy-s20-should-i-buy\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">something we're seeing yet again with the S20</a>.</p> \n   <p>There are five available colors this time around, including Cloud Blue, Cloud Pink, Cosmic Grey, Cosmic Black, and a Best Buy exclusive in the form of Aura Blue. There's nothing as extravagant as the Galaxy Note 10's Aura Glow, but the colors that are offered all look great.</p> \n   <p>Cloud Blue and Cloud Pink are have a pleasing pastel feeling that allows them to stand out without being overbearing, with Cosmic Grey and Cosmic Black existing for folks that like to keep things as simple as possible. Aura Blue is also a sight to behold, but it's not the easiest to get your hands on.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"accessories\">You'll want some accessories, and these are the best ones</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/samsung-galaxy-s20\" title=\"Samsung Galaxy S20: Everything you need to know!\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large_wm_brw/public/article_images/2020/02/samsung-galaxy-s20-cases-9.jpg?itok=FjjeBm9u\" /></a></p> \n   <p>The Galaxy S20 is a phenomenal phone on its own, but it's not something that should be used naked. A screen protector is a must to keep its jaw-dropping display intact, while a case will ensure the phone doesn't get ruined during a drop/fall.</p> \n   <p>There are also other types of accessories to consider for your shiny new phone, such as microSD cards, wireless chargers, and more.</p> \n   <p>If you want to make sure you get the most out of your S20, check out our roundups of the very best 01:31:29","updatedTime":"2020-09-01 01:31:29","title":"OnePlus explains why it moved away from stock Android","link":"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/androidcentral/~3/TdMxNDF0mgU/oneplus-explains-why-it-moved-away-stock-android-design","description":"<div class=\"field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden\"><div class=\"field-items\"><div class=\"field-item even\"><p class=\"intro\">\"Stock Android is a good starting point for mobile devices, but we also believe there's a lot we can do to make the experience even better.\"</p>\n\n<div class=\"article-body__video\"><div class=\"video_iframe\"><iframe src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/s9uFLWqnH8A?modestbranding=0&#38;html5=1&#38;rel=0&#38;autoplay=0&#38;wmode=opaque&#38;loop=0&#38;controls=1&#38;autohide=0&#38;showinfo=0&#38;theme=dark&#38;color=red&#38;enablejsapi=1\" width=\"682\" height=\"400\" class=\"video-filter video-youtube vf-s9uflwqnh8a\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"true\" loading=\"lazy\"></iframe></div></div>\n\n<!--/video-->\n\n<h2 class=\"aside news-summary\">What you need to know</h2>\n\n<ul class=\"end\">\n<li>OnePlus is moving OxygenOS away from a stock Android design to one that hews more closely towards Samsung's OneUI.</li>\n<li>The company says the move is part of a desire to improve stock Android.</li>\n<li>OxygenOS's redesign is intended to improve one-hand usability on large devices, a space the company says Google's own software isn't good at.</li>\n</ul>\n\n<p>OxygenOS is getting a redesign with version 11, and it has proved to be controversial with fans. The software is moving away from what one could see as a system inspired by Google's stock Android to one that more closely resembles other Android OEMs.</p>\n\n<p>OnePlus today shared the reasoning behind that, <a href=\"https://forums.oneplus.com/threads/a-peek-inside-oxygenos-11.1291271/\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">writing on their official forums</a>:</p>\n\n<blockquote>\n  <p>As screens increase in size, so does the unused white space. We wanted to make the most of that space while keeping the interface easy to use. We conducted A/B testing with our users to determine the best size of the headline, and found that 65% prefer slightly smaller headlines. Also, 80% of users tested preferred titles with subtitles rather than without. The result is a new headline-body hierarchy that streamlines information delivery in OxygenOS 11.</p>\n</blockquote>\n\n<p>The company further noted that the changes were also being done to adapt Android to one-handed mobile use:</p>\n\n<blockquote>\n  <p>We also know that stock Android hasn't been optimized for one-handed usage on a larger display, so we set out to make it easier for you to use. We analyzed how people use phones and looked at anthropometric data to design a UI for more comfortable one-handed use.</p>\n  \n  <p>Since people hold their phones at the bottom, it's naturally more difficult to reach the top of the phone. The updated layout of OxygenOS 11 now moves the touch controls closer to your thumbs for easier access as soon as you open a menu.</p>\n</blockquote>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/oneplus-explains-why-it-moved-away-stock-android-design\" title=\"OnePlus explains why it moved away from stock Android\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/article_images/2020/08/oxygenos11.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>As far as design philosophies go, it's not a novel one. <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/samsung-one-ui\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Samsung's OneUI</a> was created with the same reasoning in mind, and Huawei's EMUI magazine redesign was also built to be more suitable for one-handed use. As phones grow bigger, Google's stock Android indeed lacks many of the adaptions that OEMs have made to accommodate them — including features Apple's more restricted iOS offers.</p>\n\n<p>Despite all that, OnePlus stands to disappoint fans, many of whom have chosen it for its stock Android-like looks and even affectionately refer it as stock+. While OnePlus has never been shy about trying to improve on stock Android, some forum users have expressed that they find a visual change like this a bridge too far.</p>\n\n<h3 class=\"category The field of view is slightly smaller than on the Ring Video Doorbell 3, but that shouldn't make too much of a difference when it comes to most front porch spaces. While this device works on the 2.4GHz spectrum that is good for devices further from your router, you won't be able to take advantage of the faster speeds of your 5GHz network.</p>\n\n<h3 class=\"pros\">Pros:</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Most affordable Ring doorbell</li>\n<li>1080p recording and night vision</li>\n<li>Improved privacy zones and audio privacy</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h3 class=\"cons\">Cons:</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>No infrared night vision</li>\n<li>Requires subscription to access recordings</li>\n</ul>\n\n<!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h2 class=\"category reco-block\">Best Budget Doorbell</h2>\n\n<h3 class=\"product\">Ring Video Doorbell (2nd Gen)</h3>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/best-smart-doorbells-support-alexa\" title=\"Best Smart Doorbells That <em>Arlo Video Doorbell</em></h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/best-smart-doorbells-support-alexa\" title=\"Best Smart Doorbells That Support Alexa 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/article_images/2020/02/arlo-video-doorbell-lifestyle.jpg?itok=vmy0hRMf\"></a></p>\n\n<p>Arlo devices typically do well in our security camera roundups because they are feature-packed for a fair price. The Arlo Video Doorbell brings a lot of the same great capabilities as some of the others on this list and bests them in one key area: field of view.</p>\n\n<p>The Arlo Video Doorbell has a 180-degree field of view and records at a 1:1 aspect ratio instead of 16:9 like most video doorbells. This means that you get to see more above and below your subject, while still seeing a lot of the side to side.</p>\n\n<p>Arlo takes that concept of seeing more even further by building in what it calls Foresight, or pre-roll recording to the device. This lets you see what happens from the moment motion is detected up to the point where the button is pressed, and the video is recorded.</p>\n\n<p>While it's unfortunate that you can't record locally, like with other Arlo cameras, you do get the benefit of three months of Arlo's Smart cloud storage. After those three months are up, you'll have to pay for the <a href=\"https://www.arlo.com/en-us/landing/arlosmart/\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">subscription</a> if you want to be able to access your recordings.</p>\n\n<h3 class=\"pros\">Pros:</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>180-degree field of view</li>\n<li>1080p HDR video</li>\n<li>Arlo Foresight pre-roll footage</li>\n<li>1:1 aspect ratio</li>\n<li>Three months of Arlo Smart included</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h3 class=\"cons\">Cons:</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Need subscription to access recordings </li>\n<li>Can't store video locally </li>\n</ul>\n\n<!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h2 class=\"category reco-block\">Best View</h2>\n\n<h3 class=\"product\">Arlo Video Doorbell</h3>\n\n<p><a Pro</em></h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/best-smart-doorbells-support-alexa\" title=\"Best Smart Doorbells That Support Alexa 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/article_images/2019/11/august-doorbell-cam-pro-official-lifestyle.png?itok=pEPIa1dX\"></a></p>\n\n<p>August is a smart home devices company that has built a solid reputation for itself, particularly when it comes to smart door products. The August smart locks are some of the most advanced and highest-rated around, so it should come as no surprise that it offers one of my favorite smart doorbell devices: the August Doorbell Cam Pro.</p>\n\n<p>A major reason that you might elect to go with this doorbell over others is its integration with August's smart locks. You can easily let friends or family into your home remotely through the app or via Alexa. Installing this device might present some headaches for the non-technical, as it only comes in a wired version, and its unusual shape (square vs. rectangle) might present some mounting challenges. This thing just looks cool. While some of the doorbells from Ring, Nest, and others have a very utilitarian look and feel to them, this beauty from August looks like a doorbell from the future.</p>\n\n<p>The 960x1280 camera has the convenience of a built-in, motion-activated floodlight so that it can record full-color HD footage, even at night. It has a narrower field of view than some of the competition, which might not make it ideal for wide porches or for viewing your full front yard. August generously offers up to 24 hours of free video storage with its basic subscription, which comes included with the purchase of your Doorbell cam. However, to get more storage, you'll need to sign up for its <a href=\"https://support.august.com/about-august-video-recording-subscriptions-H1MvUkR_G\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Premium or Premium Plus options</a>, which are still a good bargain.</p>\n\n<h3 class=\"pros\">Pros:</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Full HD camera with built-in floodlight</li>\n<li>Free video may not be familiar to you, but you probably know its parent company, Anker, which also makes products that work with Alexa. The eufy Video Doorbell is a great value for many reasons, including its quality hardware specs and its great storage solution.</p>\n\n<p>This doorbell has a wide-angle field of view, a motion-activated camera that can record five seconds before the initial alert you receive, and it can record 2K HD video for clearer playback. Speaking of video playback, the eufy Video Doorbell comes with 4GB of local storage secured with 256-bit military-grade encryption, so your footage stays on-site and secure. Eufy does not charge any monthly or annual fees to access that storage. The device is also IP65 water-resistant and has a 180-day battery life.</p>\n\n<p>As with most of these smart cameras, the eufy Video Doorbell allows you to interact with visitors through the app or via Alexa, but perhaps the coolest feature is that you can set up pre-recorded responses for when you're unavailable or \"unavailable.\" You can program the doorbell to tell the delivery person to \"just leave it on the porch, please.\"</p>\n\n<p>Since this doorbell requires a wired connection and may not work with existing chimes, professional installation may be recommended for some folks who might not be handy. It's also worth noting that many have called into question the accuracy of eufy's person/motion detection features, saying that they get more false positives than expected. If you have shrubs or trees near the front door, this is something you may want to keep in mind.</p>\n\n<h3 class=\"pros\">Pros:</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>Wireless chime included</li>\n<li>Free storage with doorbell is best for renters, but really it's great for anyone who has a solid door with a peephole in it (or space for a peephole). With minimal installation, you get three products in one device — a doorbell, a peephole, and a camera. Now that's value!</p>\n\n<p>Ring has done a great job in creating a product that even a layperson like me can install easily (and without wires!), and it included most of its best tech smarts in the process. That being said, if your door doesn't already have a peephole, you'll have to physically drill one. If that describes your situation, then this may not be the best option for you.</p>\n\n<p>This doorbell features a 1080p HD video camera that allows you to interact with people at your doorstep through your Alexa device or in the Ring app. The camera doesn't record HDR video, and while the field of view is still better than most, it's slightly lower than the Ring Video Doorbell 2. Recordings are triggered by a motion sensor that you can customize to set motion zones and only receive notifications if those areas are activated.</p>\n\n<p>One cool feature that the Peephole Cam offers that no other Ring Doorbell can claim is Knock Detection. Because this device is located where the peephole is and not where a traditional doorbell would be, some visitors may not know that you do have a doorbell. So if they simply knock on the door out of habit, you'll still get a notification that you have a guest just like you would if they press the doorbell button. <em>Insert your knock-knock jokes here Alexa.</em></p>\n\n<h3 class=\"pros\">Pros:</h3>\n\n<ul>\n<li>HD video recording</li>\n<li>Passthrough peephole </li>\n<li>Knock detection feature</li>\n<li>Same great smart features as found on other aren't looking to spend a lot of money, but you still want some smart functionality for your doorbell. Maybe you don't have an Echo Show or Fire TV and can't easily look at the video feeds without opening an app on your phone <em>like an animal</em>. Whatever the case, we have a solution for you in the Arlo Audio Doorbell.</p>\n\n<p>With the Arlo Audio Doorbell, you can still utilize Alexa's services to interact with visitors through your Echo or Echo Dot by using your voice. Perhaps, even more interesting is how visitors can record messages for you through the device, which you can listen to remotely or at your leisure.</p>\n\n<p>As mentioned above, this doorbell does not feature a camera. Still, you can connect it to an existing Arlo smart camera to get the same benefits as some of the more premium video doorbells. Alternatively, you can start with just the Audio Doorbell and pick up an Arlo smart camera at a later date to save money in the near term. Another potential drawback to this device is that it requires a smart hub, which you'll have to purchase separately if you want it to work with Alexa.</p>\n\n<h3 class=\"separator\">Alexa, who's at the door?</h2>\n\n<p>I'm on record as saying that a smart doorbell is one of the most useful smart home devices that you can get for your home. Whether you use it because you're a lazy couch potato like me, or you appreciate the added safety feature of knowing who is on your property if you're home alone, a smart doorbell is a sound investment in home security.</p>\n\n<p>If you are even a casual user of Alexa and <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/best-alexa-device\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Alexa devices</a>, then I recommend you get one of the great products from Ring like the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Staging-Product-Not-Retail-Sale/dp/B0849J7W5X/ref=sr_1_1_sspa?tag=androidcentralb-20&#38;ascsubtag=UUacUdUnU82037YYr\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Ring Video Doorbell 3</a>. This device gives you full HD video, affordable storage plans, and excellent Alexa integration.</p>\n\n<p>If Ring isn't for you, there are plenty of other great smart doorbell manufacturers with products that work well with Alexa, like August, eufy, and Arlo. Regardless of your style, budget, or preference, there is bound to be a great option for you on this list.</p>\n\n<h2 class=\"no-amazon\">Credits — The team that worked on this guide</h2>\n\n<p class=\"credit\"><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/best-smart-doorbells-support-alexa\" title=\"Best Smart Doorbells That Support Alexa 2020\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/article_images/2019/09/jeramy-johnson.jpg?itok=hsg0Owws\"></a></p>\n\n<p class=\"end\"><strong>Jeramy Johnson</strong> is proud to help to Keep Austin Weird and loves hiking in the hill country of central Texas with a breakfast taco in each hand. Based in the British Virgin Islands, the company started back in 2009 and prides itself on operating a no logging policy meaning data is kept super secure.</p>\n\n<p>In 2017, one of the company's servers was used to delete information related to a Russian ambassador assasination. Despite the server being seized and searched, no information was found. The company used this as an example to show that its level of privacy was superb. It did recognise that it can be used negatively but also stated it still stands for our right to privacy and freedom online.</p>\n\n<p>At the time of publishing ExpressVPN sports an impressive 3,000 servers that span 94 countries and 160 locations across the planet.</p>\n\n<h2>Pricing and plans</h2>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.xvtelink.com%2Foffer%2Fandroidcentral%3Furl%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.expressvpn.com%252Ftechradar%26offer%3D3monthsfree%26a_fid%3D744%26data1%3DUUacUdUnU87106YYr&#38;token=yavJwLhL\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"></a><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/expressvpn-review\" title=\"ExpressVPN Review\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/article_images/2020/03/expressvpn-pricing.png\"></a></p>\n\n<p>ExpressVPN keeps pricing pretty easy to understand with <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.xvtelink.com%2Foffer%2Fandroidcentral%3Furl%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.expressvpn.com%252Forder%26offer%3D3monthsfree%26a_fid%3D744%26data1%3DUUacUdUnU87106YYr&#38;token=fzmBTIqq\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">three tiers</a>. If you want to make a saving and are willing to commit to a longer term contract then you can pay for six months at $9.99 per month. This is billed every six months at $59.94.</p>\n\n<p>The best savings comes from purchasing the annual plan, which comes in at $99.95 for the period. Of course if you do want to try that month even that's technically free as you have a 30-day money-back guarantee. You don't need a reason to cancel, there isn't any smallprint and all you need to do is tell ExpressVPN and you'll get your money back.</p>\n\n<h2>Testing and performance</h2>\n\n<p>One of the best ways to test a VPN is on performance, which means speed. This is easily done using a speed test site – even Google has one right there on its search site now. We used this and other speed test sites to assess just how fast the servers are running.</p>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/expressvpn-review\" title=\"ExpressVPN Review\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/article_images/2020/03/expressvpn-speed-tests.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>Our tests initially run across two locations – the U.S. and the UK. We then test other locations, like Asia, Australia and Africa, with benchmarking sites to see how fast they run over longer distances.</p>\n\n<p>For the US we used a 400MB line and ran multiple tests using different locations. To start, we ran a speed test with no VPN enabled. That's the top result shown on the right. The second one is using the \"Smart Server\" location, and the third one was a server based in Singapore. As you can see, the speeds do drop off the further away the connections are, but they are still reasonable, and are actually some of the best we've experienced in our testing.</p>\n\n<p>In the UK the testing line was a 75Mbps connection. The results were 60 to 65Mbps which was very impressive when you consider how near the top-end of that line's capacity this reached.</p>\n\n<p>From the UK as a base, connecting to the likes of Hong Kong, India or Australia we were getting speeds of a decent 60Mbps. Go to Brazil or Kenya and the results suffered with the top-end hitting nearer to the 20Mbps mark.</p>\n\n<h2>Features</h2>\n\n<p>The mighty 3,000 servers of ExpressVPN, spanning those 94 countries and 160 locations worldwide mean you can appear to be from virtually anywhere you need. The key with this many server locations is that you should always be relatively close to one so you can enjoy a fast and consistent connection speed.</p>\n\n<p>This VPN masking applies to lots of devices as well as locations. This is thanks to the clients available which span the likes of Mac, Windows, iOS, Linux, Android Chromebooks, Kindle Fire, PlayStation, Apple TV, Fire TV and more. You can also setup the VPN on a router using custom firmware. So, despite ExpressVPN limiting you to five devices used at one time, if one of them is a router that means you can connect as many devices to that as you need.</p>\n\n<p>Getting the apps up and running is super easy. It takes just a few minutes to <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/how-download-and-install-expressvpn-android\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">install ExpressVPN on your Android</a> device. The interface is very simple to understand and makes it something you'll actually want to use regularly instead of something you uninstall quickly.</p>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/expressvpn-review\" title=\"ExpressVPN Review\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/article_images/2020/03/expressvpn-dashboard.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p>ExpressVPN uses all its own secure servers meaning you can enjoy that no-logging as well as encryption storage so your data is safe in transit too. The company's relatively new TrustedServer Technology uses RAM to process information meaning none of your data is stored on hard drives at any time, making it even more difficult to get hold of. Also, everytime you connect to a new network, that's not trusted, ExpressVPN will fire up automatically to offer protection. Connect to a secure network again and ExpressVPN will close down so you can get top speeds as your priority.</p>\n\n<p>One of the most stand out ExpressVPN features is the 24/7 live chat support. This means you can get help with literally any issues you have – presuming it's ExpressVPN related, of course. Say you're trying to connect to Netflix while abroad but can't, the experts are there to help you find the best server so you not only get access but can enjoy the fastest speeds for what you're doing too.</p>\n\n<p>Since you can access most locations, that means you can get to most content too. For streaming the likes of Netflix, Hulu or even BBC iPlayer, this is a really decent VPN. We even got the chance to test this while in China. Initially we struggled to get access to US Netflix so we got on the 24/7 live chat. We were told exactly what server to connect to and right away we were up and running at great speed.</p>\n\n<h2>Privacy and security</h2>\n\n<p>ExpressVPN runs an encryption service across its offerings meaning 4096-bit SHA-512 RAS certificate level cover. This uses AES-256-CBC to encrypt and HMAC protection too. There's also support for Perfect Forward Secrecy meaning you get a new secret key every time you connect.</p>\n\n<p>All that is complicated tech-speak for a super encryption. It's as good as, if not better than most other VPN options out there with a few exceptions that offer double hop encryption for yet another layer of protection.</p>\n\n<p>Another highlight is DNS support in the form of DNS leak protection to stop information leaking from the tunnel while in transit. Lots of VPNs offer this but ExpressVPN goes further by running its own zero-knowledge, 256-bit encrypted DNS on all of its servers too. That essentially means you don't have to worry about attackers getting to you or your data.</p>\n\n<p>You also get a kill switch so, should you lose connection, you'll automatically be protected and hidden then too.</p>\n\n<p>The clear lack of logging is also a great way to leave your mind at ease. The company clearly states on its site: \"ExpressVPN does not and will never log traffic data, DNS queries, or anything that could be used to identify you.\"</p>\n\n<p>The British Virgin Island location helps since, despite its small size, the country regulates its own affairs. That means the UK and US don't have jurisdiction to automatically compel ExpressVPN to release any data.</p>\n\n<h2>Should you sign up?</h2>\n\n<p>ExpressVPN has a lot to like. Beyond the wide spread servers across the world there are the layers and layers of security and encryption backed by a clear no logging policy which combine to give you peace of mind security, anonymity and safety when online.</p>\n\n<p>The pricing is competitive, support is superb and performance speeds are excellent. The only downside is that you're limited to five devices, but with the ability to install this on routers that can be worked around.</p>\n\n<p>This is a tough VPN to fault. If you want even more security there are other double hop options out there and some with more servers but it's hard to find a service with a track record like ExpressVPN. A device by the name of \"OnePlus Watch\" <a href=\"https://www.91mobiles.com/hub/oneplus-watch-revealed-by-imda-certification-may-launch-soon/\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">went through Indonesia's IMDA</a> on that date, which is the country's equivalent of the FCC here in the United States.</p> \n   <p>That suggests that the OnePlus Watch is getting very close to its eventual launch date, and when you add that together with <a href=\"https://www.techradar.com/news/oneplus-watch-name-leaks-as-ex-employee-reveals-its-been-in-the-works-for-a-while\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">another report from <em>TechRadar</em></a> that OnePlus has \"actively been looking into a smartwatch for the last year,\" the time is right for the wearable to finally drop.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"price\">How much is the OnePlus Watch going to cost?</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/oneplus-watch\" title=\"OnePlus Watch: News, Leaks, Release Date, Specs, and Rumors!\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large_wm_brw/public/article_images/2018/09/oneplus-logo.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>If you don't know by now, OnePlus has a very close relationship with OPPO in the sense that both brands are owned and operated by BBK Electronics in China. New OnePlus smartphones are often slight deviations of OPPO handsets that come out before them, and in the case of the OnePlus Watch, we're expecting it to be a lot like the recently-released <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/oppos-wear-os-powered-smartwatch-launching-july-31\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">OPPO Watch</a>.</p> \n   <p>The OPPO Watch goes for ₹14,990 in India, which is about $205 USD. This means we should be able to look forward to a relatively low price when the OnePlus Watch launches in the United States, hopefully around that $200 marker.</p> \n   <p>Samsung's <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/samsung-galaxy-watch-3-review\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Galaxy Watch 3</a>, by comparison, starts at $400 at the lowest and goes up to $480 for the most expensive model. Even if the OnePlus Watch hits $250 or $300, it'll still have that price advantage in its favor.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"design\">What does the OnePlus Watch look like?</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/oneplus-watch\" title=\"OnePlus Watch: News, Leaks, Release Date, Specs, and Rumors!\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large_wm_brw/public/article_images/2020/08/oppo-watch-17_0.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>Not only does OnePlus's close relationship with OPPO give us a good idea of what the Watch could cost, it also provides a pretty clear picture as to what the OnePlus Watch is going to look like.</p> \n   <p>The OPPO Watch (pictured above) has a design that takes a lot of inspiration from the Apple Watch. It has a square body with rounded corners, minimal bezels around the screen, and watch bands that flow perfectly into the frame with no visible lugs.</p> \n   <p>Mock or make fun of it if you want, but it's an effective design that works well for both form and functionality. You can fit more text on a square display than you can on a circular one, and thanks to the minimal aesthetics, the OPPO Watch fits the part of a fitness accessory or something you wear to a nice dinner.</p> \n   <p>OnePlus could take some liberties with the case and watchband colors to make the design more of its own, but don't expect anything drastically different in this department.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"specs\">What specs will the OnePlus Watch have?</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/oneplus-watch\" title=\"OnePlus Watch: News, Leaks, Release Date, Specs, and Rumors!\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large_wm_brw/public/article_images/2020/08/oppo-watch-13.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>Just like the price and design, specs for the OnePlus Watch should also be virtually identical compared to the OPPO Watch. If you're in the market for a <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/best-android-smartwatch\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Wear OS watch</a> right now and don't feel like waiting, one of the better ones you can get in 2020 is the Fossil Gen 5.</p> \n   <p>The Fossil Gen 5 offers a solid Wear OS experience, giving you a classic round design with ample features to back it up. There's built-in GPS, NFC for Google Pay, 3ATM water resistance, and a speaker for taking hands-free phone calls directly on the watch. In terms of specs, you're looking at a Snapdragon Wear 3100, 1GB of RAM, and 8GB of storage for all of your apps.</p> \n   <p>Given the nature of Wear OS and how companies aren't allowed to heavily customize it the way they can for Android, the experience you get on the Fossil Gen 5 is very similar to what should be offered on the OnePlus Watch. news-summary\">What you need to know</h2>\n\n<ul class=\"end\">\n<li>Google has introduced Kids Space for Android tablets.</li>\n<li>It's a child-friendly interface aimed at highlighting content It has YouTube Kids and <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/how-set-screen-time-limits-google-family-link\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Family Link</a>, it's <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/google-makes-it-easier-find-teacher-approved-kid-friendly-apps-play-store\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">also introduced a teacher-approved section of the Play Store</a> to keep children learning at home. Now. it's taking all these efforts to their logical conclusion and building in a new feaure — Kids Space — for Android devices. Specifically, it'll be made available on tablets.</p>\n\n<p>Once engaged, it'll enable a colorful interface showcasing a selection of child-friendly media ranging from games to videos to books to apps. Google says this mode will only come on certain tablets, like Lenovo's upcoming Smart Tab M10 HD Gen 2 tablets. For Kids Space, we've built on that foundation and applied our quality standard to an ever-expanding library of apps and books in the Play and Read tabs. We worked with top publishers to make popular children's books free of charge, and have over 400 free books available in the U.S. alone. In the Watch and Make tabs, your kids can view creative and fun videos from YouTube Kids that are engaging and encourage off-screen activities. And if you're looking to customize even more, parents can download additional content from Google Play.</p>\n</blockquote>\n\n<p>It's a lot like the <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/how-manage-parental-controls-and-use-kids-home-feature-your-samsung-galaxy-phone\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Kids Home feature</a> which Samsung offers on its Galaxy phones and tablets,albeit with a stronger content curation focus. <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/project-fi-buyers-guide\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Google Fi network</a> is how it can seamlessly switch your service between different carriers and Wi-Fi to get you the best signal possible. But you know what's better than one Google Fi network? Two Google Fi networks! We'll show you how you can use two Google Fi SIM cards to get even better network coverage.</p>\n\n<h3>Products used in this guide</h3>\n\n<ul class=\"jumplist\">\n<li>Best budget phone: <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fbestbuy.7tiv.net%2Fc%2F221109%2F615614%2F10014%3FsubId1%3DUUacUdUnU93079YYr%26subId2%3Ddac%26u%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.bestbuy.com%252Fsite%252Fgoogle-pixel-4a-128gb-unlocked-just-black%252F6422517.p&#38;token=Qj2UTZqd\" title=\"\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Google Pixel 4a</a> ($350 at Best Buy)</li>\n<li>Fi Freedom: <a href=\"https://fi.google.com/about/plans/\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Google Fi</a> (Sign up at Google Fi)</li>\n</ul>\n\n<h2 class=\"separator\">How to set up eSIM on your Pixel phone</h2>\n\n<p>For these steps, you'll need to have a stable and secure Wi-Fi connection.</p>\n\n<ol>\n<li>Open the <a href=\"https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.google.android.apps.tycho\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><strong>Google Fi app</strong></a> on your Pixel 4, 4XL, or 4a.</li>\n<li>Sign in to your <strong>Google account</strong> (remember to use a secure <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/two-factor-authentication\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">two-factor authentication</a> method!).</li>\n<li>Tap <strong>Next</strong> after you are prompted to set up your device.</li>\n<li>When you see the pop up that says your SIM will be downloaded soon, tap <strong>OK</strong>.</li>\n<li><p>You will see a landing page detailing what your Fi number is, and that your data is active. Tap <strong>Next</strong>.</p>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/you-can-use-trick-improve-google-fi-service-pixel-4-or-pixel-4a\" title=\"You can use this trick to improve Google Fi service on the Pixel 4 or Pixel 4a\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/article_images/2020/08/google-fi-set-up-esim.jpg\"></a></p></li>\n</ol>\n\n<p>Now that you've set up your Google Fi eSIM, you can use it in conjunction with the physical SIM card you received from Google Fi and switch between networks as you need to.</p>\n\n<h2>How to use two Google Fi SIMs on your Pixel phone</h2>\n\n<p>If you purchase a Pixel phone directly from Google Fi, it will come with a physical SIM card. Upon activation, that physical SIM will work in parallel with the built-in eSIM to find you the best possible wireless signal. Note that removing the physical Fi SIM will cause your phone to lose service.</p>\n\n<p>If you purchase a Pixel unlocked, and add a physical Fi SIM after you activate your Fi eSIM, follow the steps below to ensure everything works together as intended.</p>\n\n<ol>\n<li>Remove the <strong>physical SIM card</strong> from the phone.</li>\n<li>Open the <strong>Settings</strong> app.</li>\n<li>Tap <strong>Network &#38; internet</strong>.</li>\n<li>Tap <strong>Mobile Networks</strong>.</li>\n<li>Tap <strong>Google Fi</strong>.</li>\n<li><p>Tap <strong>Erase</strong>.</p>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/you-can-use-trick-improve-google-fi-service-pixel-4-or-pixel-4a\" title=\"You can use this trick to improve Google Fi service on the Pixel 4 or Pixel 4a\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/article_images/2020/08/erase-sim-google-fi.jpg\"></a></p></li>\n<li>Now, insert the <strong>physical SIM card</strong> back into the Pixel.</li>\n<li>Open the <strong>Google Fi</strong> app.</li>\n<li><p>Follow the <strong>instructions</strong> in the app to activate.</p>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/you-can-use-trick-improve-google-fi-service-pixel-4-or-pixel-4a\" title=\"You can use this trick to improve Google Fi service on the Pixel 4 or Pixel 4a\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/article_images/2020/08/google-fi-activate-sim.jpg\"></a></p></li>\n</ol>\n\n<h2>How to enable Google Fi Network Tools</h2>\n\n<ol>\n<li>Open the <strong>Google Fi app</strong>.</li>\n<li>Tap on the <strong>Account</strong> tab at the bottom left of the screen.</li>\n<li>Tap on <strong>Fi Network Tools</strong>.</li>\n<li><p>Tap to toggle on <strong>Enhance network BETA</strong>.</p>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/you-can-use-trick-improve-google-fi-service-pixel-4-or-pixel-4a\" title=\"You can use this trick to improve Google Fi service on the Pixel 4 or Pixel 4a\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/article_images/2020/08/google-fi-network-tools.jpg\"></a></p></li>\n</ol>\n\n<p>This will enable your phone to more easily switch to using mobile data when the Fi network signal is low. It also protects your traffic through Fi's virtual private network (VPN) service.</p>\n\n<h2>Our top equipment picks</h2>\n\n<p>To take advantage of this great Google Fi flexibility, be sure to pick up a <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/google-pixel-4\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Pixel 4, 4XL</a>, or <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/google-pixel-4a\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">4a</a>, and sign up for Google Fi service!</p>\n\n<!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h3 class=\"category reco-block\">Budget buddy</h3>\n\n<h4 class=\"product\">Google Pixel 4a</h4>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/you-can-use-trick-improve-google-fi-service-pixel-4-or-pixel-4a\" title=\"You can use this trick to improve Google Fi service on the Pixel 4 or Pixel 4a\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/article_images/2020/08/google-pixel-4a-product-image.jpg\"></a></p>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Google-Pixel-4a-Unlocked-Smartphone/dp/B08CFSZLQ4/ref=sr_1_3?tag=androidcentralb-20&#38;ascsubtag=UUacUdUnU93079YYr\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">$350 at Amazon</a>\n<a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fbestbuy.7tiv.net%2Fc%2F221109%2F615614%2F10014%3FsubId1%3DUUacUdUnU93079YYr%26subId2%3Ddac%26u%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.bestbuy.com%252Fsite%252Fgoogle-pixel-4a-128gb-unlocked-just-black%252F6422517.p&#38;token=Qj2UTZqd\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">$350 at Best Buy</a></p>\n\n<p class=\"subtitle\">Pocket-friendly and wallet-friendly</p>\n\n<p class=\"end\">The Pixel 4a offers the best camera you'll find in this category, and the value on offer here is staggering. You get 6GB of RAM and 128GB of storage, a clean software without any bloat, and three years of platform updates. The phone runs just fine in most day-to-day scenarios and is the ideal size for one-handed use.</p>\n\n<!-- END RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h3>Additional Equipment</h3>\n\n<p>Google's MVNO service is a fan favorite here at Android Central!</p>\n\n<div class=\"list\">\n\n<!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK -->\n\n<h3 class=\"product reco-block\">Google Fi</h3>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/you-can-use-trick-improve-google-fi-service-pixel-4-or-pixel-4a\" title=\"You can use this trick to improve Google Fi service on the Pixel 4 or Pixel 4a\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/article_images/2019/05/google-fi-logo-cropped.png\"></a></p>\n\n<p><a href=\"https://fi.google.com/about/plans/\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">Sign up at Google Fi</a></p>\n\n<p class=\"end\">Google Fi offers flexible and unlimited plans for individuals or groups of up to six people. class=\"intro\">Get ready to raid some villages and conquer new lands.</p> \n   <p>The next Assassin's Creed was revealed by Ubisoft through a livestream where graphic designer BossLogic worked some magic to create artwork for the game. As previous rumors suggested, it does take place during the time of Vikings. If the world premiere trailer is anything to go by, it promises a lot of bloody battles. Assassin's Creed Valhalla is being developed by Ubisoft Montreal, with support from 14 other studios around the world.</p> \n   <!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK --> \n   <h3 class=\"category reco-block\">Viking raids</h3> \n   <h4 class=\"product\">Assassin's Creed Valhalla</h4> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/assassins-creed-valhalla\" title=\"Assassin's Creed Valhalla on PS5: Setting, gameplay, release date, and everything you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/article_images/2020/04/assassins-creed-valhalla-ps4-box-art.jpg?itok=NO9rGzh-\" /></a></p> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B087XTT5GZ?tag=androidcentralb-20&amp;ascsubtag=UUacUdUnU89188YYr\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">$50 at Amazon</a> <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fbestbuy.7tiv.net%2Fc%2F221109%2F615614%2F10014%3FsubId1%3DUUacUdUnU89188YYr%26subId2%3Ddac%26u%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.bestbuy.com%252Fsite%252Fassassins-creed-valhalla-standard-edition-playstation-4%252F6412166.p%253FskuId%253D6412166&amp;token=5Ld6Lr7S\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">$60 at Best Buy</a> <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fgoto.walmart.com%2Fc%2F1943169%2F612734%2F9383%3Fsharedid%3D159229%26subId1%3DUUacUdUnU89188YYr%26subId2%3Ddac%26u%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.walmart.com%252Fip%252FAssassin-s-Creed-Valhalla-Ubisoft-Playstation-4-Pre-order-Bonus%252F868148643&amp;token=hq5nASwY\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">$50 at Walmart</a></p> \n   <p class=\"subtitle\">Conquer new lands for glory and honor</p> \n   <p class=\"end\">After endless wars ravage Norway and resources are scarce, you'll lead your clan to the shores of England in the hopes of finding a new home. But not everyone is keen on having Vikings around, and King Alfred of Wessex will do all he can to keep you from settling.</p> \n   <!-- END RECO-BLOCK --> \n   <!--sectionbreak:article-nav-menu narrow no-amazon mobile-always--> \n   <h3>Jump to:</h3> \n   <ul class=\"jumplist\"> \n    <li><a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/androidcentral/~3/HlOEiSkrqlE/assassins-creed-valhalla#setting\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Where and when does Valhalla take place?</a></li> \n    <li><a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/androidcentral/~3/HlOEiSkrqlE/assassins-creed-valhalla#story\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">What's the story and who are the characters?</a></li> \n    <li><a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/androidcentral/~3/HlOEiSkrqlE/assassins-creed-valhalla#gameplay\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">What's the gameplay like?</a></li> \n    <li><a href=\"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/androidcentral/~3/HlOEiSkrqlE/assassins-creed-valhalla#release\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">When does it release?</a></li> \n   </ul> \n   <!--sectionbreak--> \n   <h2 id=\"setting\"><em>Assassin's Creed Valhalla</em> Setting</h2> \n   <div class=\"article-body__video\">\n    <div class=\"video_iframe\">\n     <iframe src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/NAYrAD83iSQ?modestbranding=0&amp;html5=1&amp;rel=0&amp;autoplay=0&amp;wmode=opaque&amp;loop=0&amp;controls=1&amp;autohide=0&amp;showinfo=0&amp;theme=dark&amp;color=red&amp;enablejsapi=1\" width=\"682\" height=\"400\" class=\"video-filter video-youtube vf-nayrad83isq\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"true\" loading=\"lazy\"></iframe>\n    </div>\n   </div> \n   <!--/video--> \n   <p>Assassin's Creed Valhalla takes place during England's Dark Ages in the 9th century. According to <a href=\"https://www.gameinformer.com/2020/04/30/answers-to-our-biggest-questions-about-assassins-creed-valhalla\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Creative Director Ashraf Ismail</a>, players will visit four major English kingdoms during that time period: Wessex, Northumbria, East Anglia, and Mercia. Specific cities include London, Winchester, and Jórvík (York), along with smaller towns. Norway also plays a major role as role set sale from your homeland after endless wars. Players will be able to go back and forth between both countries.</p> \n   <p>Though Norway and England make up the core of the map, Ismail says the world still has some surprises in store that Ubisoft isn't getting into just yet.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"story\"><em>Assassin's Creed Valhalla</em> Story and characters</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/assassins-creed-valhalla\" title=\"Assassin's Creed Valhalla on PS5: Setting, gameplay, release date, and everything you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/04/assassins-creed-valhalla-image-1-aum5.jpg?itok=AoZLIEdo\" /></a></p> \n   <p>As clan leader, <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/assassins-creed-valhalla-main-character-and-setting\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Eivor (male or female)</a> will lead their clan from the war-ravaged Norway to the shores of England and beyond. Their arrival is met with resistance from King Alfred of Wessex (also known as Alfred the Great) and the Saxons, who will do everything in their power to drive you from the land. Eventually Eivor comes in contact with the Assassins during their journey, thus kicking off the age-old Assassin vs. Templar conflict the series is known for.</p> \n   <p>Ubisoft is taking inspiration from Norse mythology — much like the studio did with Egyptian and Greek mythology in Origins and Odyssey, respectively — but we don't know what role the gods will play just yet. Apparently, the lore will be more grounded than what we saw in Odyssey.</p> \n   <p>The present day story will again be playable and follow Layla Hassan from the previous two titles. Ubisoft apparently found a way to \"blend the present day into a new type of experience for players,\" but it's unclear what this means.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"gameplay\"><em>Assassin's Creed Valhalla</em> Gameplay</h2> \n   <div class=\"article-body__video\">\n    <div class=\"video_iframe\">\n     <iframe src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/YdzcijLhQV8?modestbranding=0&amp;html5=1&amp;rel=0&amp;autoplay=0&amp;wmode=opaque&amp;loop=0&amp;controls=1&amp;autohide=0&amp;showinfo=0&amp;theme=dark&amp;color=red&amp;enablejsapi=1\" width=\"682\" height=\"400\" class=\"video-filter video-youtube vf-ydzcijlhqv8\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"true\" loading=\"lazy\"></iframe>\n    </div>\n   </div> \n   <!--/video--> \n   <p>Like Assassin's Creed Odyssey before it, Valhalla will continue the series' jump into <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/assassins-creed-valhalla-rpg\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">RPG territory</a>. Players in Valhalla will be able to forge political alliances and choose dialogue options that will affect the story. A revamped combat system now allows players to dual-wield any combination of weapons (including two shields) against a \"greater variety of enemies than ever before.\" Whether you want to brutally decapitate them with a war axe or stealthily kill them in the shadows with your <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/will-hidden-blade-return-assassins-creed-valhalla\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">hidden blade (it's back!)</a>, the choice is yours. This is all about nailing that visceral feeling of being a Viking warrior.</p> \n   <p>It seems like Ubisoft heard complaints loud and clear, because some penchants from the earlier Assassin's Creed games are returning. Not only is the hidden blade back, but it can also be upgraded so that you can instakill just about anyone, just like the good old days. Social stealth is also making a return, though it's unclear just how our viking warrior will be blending into the crowds. And when a fan asked if there would be any tombs in Valhalla, <a href=\"https://twitter.com/DarbyMcDevitt/status/1260582475396505600\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Lead Writer Darby McDevitt teased</a> that there are \"many buried secrets.\"</p> \n   <blockquote class=\"pull left\"> \n    <p>Not only is the hidden blade back, but it can also be upgraded so that you can instakill just about anyone.</p> \n   </blockquote> \n   <p>New features include raids, settlement growing, and the ability expand your power and influence. With raids, you can pillage enemy villages and fortresses across England for valuable resources. Settlement growing appears to be like what Assassin's Creed 2 and Brotherhood offered with Monteriggioni and Rome, but greatly expanded with more depth. Players can construct and upgrade barracks, blacksmiths, tattoo parlors, and more.</p> \n   <p>One such settlement will serve as a hub for the player. \"It's at the center of our quests and the center of the decisions you make. We want players to see the consequences of their actions,\" Lead Producer Julien Laferrière told <a href=\"https://www.eurogamer.net/articles/2020-04-30-assassins-creed-valhalla-reshapes-the-series-rpg-storytelling-by-giving-you-a-viking-settlement\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Eurogamer</a>.</p> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/assassins-creed-valhalla\" title=\"Assassin's Creed Valhalla on PS5: Setting, gameplay, release date, and everything you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/04/assassins-creed-valhalla-image-2-dohv.jpg\" /></a></p> \n   <p>\"It really changed the shape of the game we were making,\" Laferrière said. \"Instead of exploring one territory, then moving on to another and having no real opportunity or reason to return, the settlement changes the structure. So you'll go on an adventure and then be encouraged to come back to your settlement. It changes the way we're playing the game we're making - at least, that's the bet we're making.\"</p> \n   <p>In a first for the series, players can create customize a unique Viking raider and share it online with friends who can then use it during their own raids (though there is so co-op or multiplayer in Valhalla). Players will also be able to customize hair, tattoos, war paint and gear of their own character. Gear can be upgraded throughout the game so that a set of weapons or armor you begin the game with will still feel formidable as you progress.</p> \n   <div class=\"article-body__video\">\n    <div class=\"video_iframe\">\n     <iframe src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/sGyM5Xh7Jf0?modestbranding=0&amp;html5=1&amp;rel=0&amp;autoplay=0&amp;wmode=opaque&amp;loop=0&amp;controls=1&amp;autohide=0&amp;showinfo=0&amp;theme=dark&amp;color=red&amp;enablejsapi=1\" width=\"682\" height=\"400\" class=\"video-filter video-youtube vf-sgym5xh7jf0\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"true\" loading=\"lazy\"></iframe>\n    </div>\n   </div> \n   <!--/video--> \n   <blockquote class=\"pull right\"> \n    <p>Ravens are largely associated with the Norse god Odin.</p> \n   </blockquote> \n   <p>Instead of your trusty pet eagle to help guide you along your journey and act as some eyes in the sky, a raven will be filling that role in Assassin's Creed Valhalla. After all, ravens are largely associated with the Norse god Odin.</p> \n   <p>\"We have a bunch of new abilities for the raven,\" Laferrière said. \"We used it as a reason to re-explore the way players can explore the world so it is less reliant on UI. If you notice a distraction somewhere it's probably because there's some content there.\"</p> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/does-assassins-creed-valhalla-have-naval-combat\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Naval gameplay</a> will be a major element as well, but don't expect to be fighting on the sea often. Vikings are known for being fearsome warriors, and many battles were won because of their skills as sailors, but they didn't partake in naval combat like you'd expect. The Vikings longship will play a crucial role in traversing the map and bringing your raiding party where it needs to go. Ismail teases a lot of surprises in store with the longship, but he did not go into detail.</p> \n   <p>The company revealed that for the first time ever, players will be able to <a href=\"https://www.ign.com/articles/assassins-creed-valhalla-gender-eivor-animus?sf125224448=1\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">switch between male and female Eivor</a> whenever they'd like in the menu, meaning both genders are canonical to the story, though the reasoning for why this is possible was not explained. Players will also be able to play as Layla in the open-world of England. Previously, modern day characters could not be played in the historical simulation.</p> \n   <h2 id=\"release\"><em>Assassin's Creed Valhalla</em> Release date and platforms</h2> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/assassins-creed-valhalla\" title=\"Assassin's Creed Valhalla on PS5: Setting, gameplay, release date, and everything you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/field/image/2020/04/assassins_creed_valhalla_7-1vozr.jpg?itok=6PR2-Ffu\" /></a></p> \n   <p>Assassin's Creed Valhalla will release November 17, 2020 for Xbox One, Xbox Series X, PlayStation 4, <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/playstation-5\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">PS5</a>, PC (Epic Games Store and Uplay), and Stadia. You can pre-order it now.</p> \n   <p>For anyone worrying about which Microsoft console to buy it for, it will support Xbox Smart Delivery, meaning that one purchase gets you the game on both Xbox One and Xbox Series X. It will run at 4K on Microsoft's upcoming platform. It is unknown what resolutions it will run at on Sony's consoles or if you can buy one copy for both PS4 and PS5.</p> \n   <!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK --> \n   <h3 class=\"category reco-block\">Viking raids</h3> \n   <h4 class=\"product\">Assassin's Creed Valhalla</h4> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/assassins-creed-valhalla\" title=\"Assassin's Creed Valhalla on PS5: Setting, gameplay, release date, and everything you need to know\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\"><img src=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/sites/androidcentral.com/files/styles/large/public/article_images/2020/04/assassins-creed-valhalla-ps4-box-art.jpg?itok=NO9rGzh-\" /></a></p> \n   <p><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B087XTT5GZ?tag=androidcentralb-20&amp;ascsubtag=UUacUdUnU89188YYr\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">$50 at Amazon</a> <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fbestbuy.7tiv.net%2Fc%2F221109%2F615614%2F10014%3FsubId1%3DUUacUdUnU89188YYr%26subId2%3Ddac%26u%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.bestbuy.com%252Fsite%252Fassassins-creed-valhalla-standard-edition-playstation-4%252F6412166.p%253FskuId%253D6412166&amp;token=5Ld6Lr7S\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">$60 at Best Buy</a> <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/e?link=https%3A%2F%2Fgoto.walmart.com%2Fc%2F1943169%2F612734%2F9383%3Fsharedid%3D159229%26subId1%3DUUacUdUnU89188YYr%26subId2%3Ddac%26u%3Dhttps%253A%252F%252Fwww.walmart.com%252Fip%252FAssassin-s-Creed-Valhalla-Ubisoft-Playstation-4-Pre-order-Bonus%252F868148643&amp;token=hq5nASwY\" title=\"\" class=\"cta shop norewrite\" rel=\"nofollow\" georiot-ignore=\"true\">$50 at Walmart</a></p> \n   <p class=\"subtitle\">Conquer new lands for glory and honor</p> \n   <p class=\"end\">After endless wars ravage Norway and resources are scarce, you'll lead your clan to the shores of England in the hopes of finding a new home. But not everyone is keen on having Vikings around, and King Alfred of Wessex will do all he can to keep you from settling.</p> \n   <!-- END RECO-BLOCK -->\n  </div>\n </div>\n</div>\n<img Given the custom architecture of the PS3, support has always seemed unlikely.</p>\n\n<p>Now, a major publisher has given a definitive statement on the subject. Valhalla</a>, <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/far-cry-6\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Far Cry 6</a> and <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/watch-dogs-legion-playstation-4\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">Watch Dogs: Legion</a>, support free upgrades, meaning you can buy the game on PS4 and get the PS5 version at no extra cost.</p>\n\n<p>You can also use a DualShock 4 controller with the PS5 when playing PS4 games, though you'll need to use the new <a href=\"https://www.androidcentral.com/does-playstation-5-controller-use-usb-c-charging\" georiot-ignore=\"true\" class=\"norewrite\">DualSense</a> when playing PS5 titles.</p>\n\n<!-- BEGIN RECO-BLOCK
